10th May 2019.	
Registrar,
	
Tamil Nadu Siddha Medical Council.
(Ref. No.32 / TNSMC / 2019.)
No.32- 2019 - Whereas the Tamil Nadu Siddha Medical Council is maintaining a register as the State Register of Siddha Medicine which contains the 
names of persons enrolled on the State Register of Siddha of Tamil Nadu and who posses any of the Medical qualifications recognised under Indian Medicine 
Central Council Act, 1970.
The Register shall be deemed to be a public document within the meaning of Indian Evidence Act, 1872 (1 of 1872) and may be proved by a copy published 
in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette.
Note : While every care has been taken to compile the State Register of Siddha, ommission / Correction, if any, be reported to the Registrar, Tamil Nadu 
Siddha Medical Council, Arignar Anna Government Hospital of Indian Medicine Campus, Arumbakkam, Chennai - 600 106 for rectification of the same in the 
next publication of the Register.
	
G. RAJASEKARAN,
Chennai- 600 106.	
Registrar,	
	
	
	
	
10th May 2019.	
Tamil Nadu Siddha Medical Council.
